# Stored genus-2 ribbon graph data with two faces
# How to read this file:
# - Topology N is the N-th ribbon graph returned by generate_ribbon_graphs_fixed_genus(2, n_faces=2).
# - Each topology here has genus 2 and exactly 2 faces.
# - edges = ((edge_label, vertex_a, vertex_b), ...).
# - face_boundaries = (face_1, face_2) where each face is listed counterclockwise
#   as ((from_vertex, to_vertex, edge_label), ...).
# - face_edge_sequences and face_vertex_sequences list the edge labels and starting
#   vertices around each face, respectively.
# - gluing_pairs = ((edge_label, face1, pos1, face2, pos2), ...) means the half-edge
#   at position pos1 of face1 is glued to the half-edge at position pos2 of face2
#   with opposite orientation to form edge edge_label.
# - All labels and face/position indices are 1-based integers.
